 ) chakravarti rajagopalchaari kaa janm madras ke thorpalli gaanv main 10 disambar 1878 ko hua tha
 Rojagopalachari is also known as Rajaji
 unhone madras college se lau kii degree hasil kii thi
 Rajagopalachari was one of the prominent leaders of the Congress and was considered very close to Mahatma Gandhi
 1930 main jab gandhi ji ne dandi march kiya to inhone bhi namak kanoon todaa tha
 Along with politics, Rajagopalachari also deeply hurt the kitsch of Indian caste
 kai mandiron main jahaan dalit samudaay kaa mandir main janaa varjit tha, inhone is niyam kaa datakar virodh kiya
 Due to this, the entry of Dalits into the temples was possible
 1938 main inhone agriculture date relif act kanoon banaaya taaki kisaanon ko karj se raahat mil sake
 Rajagopalachari was also elected as the General Secretary of the Congress
 antim governor mountbeton ke baad rajagopalchaari bharat ke pehle governor bane the
 He was also made the Home Minister in the Jawaharlal Nehru-led government in 1950
 1952 main rajagopalchaari ne madras ke mukhyamantri ke rup main thapath lee
 He was awarded the Bharat Ratna in 1954, India's best civilian award, for serving the country from the freedom struggle onwards
 baad main nehru se apni vaicharik asahmati ke kaaran congress se alag ho gaye
 Separating from the Congress, he formed his own separate party, which was named 'anti Congress Swatantra Party'
 raajnneetik kaamon ke alaava inhone sanskrit granth 'ramayana' kaa tamil main anuwaad kiya
 Rajagopalachari was an excellent writer of Tamil as well as English
 inhone salem litereri socity ke sansthaapak the

 History of Muzaffarnagar seat The Congress dominated the Lok Sabha seat for many years
 1952 ke pehle loksabhaa chunaav se lekar 1962 tak ye seat congress ke khate main hi rahi, jiske baad lagaataar do baar communist party of india ne jeet darj kii thi
 From 1977 to 1991, this seat was in the account of Janata Dal, Congress
 1990 ke aasapaas jab desh main ram mandir kaa mudda charam par tha to uskaa asar yahaan bhi dekhne ko mila
 In the 1991, 1996 and 1998 Lok Sabha elections, the Bharatiya Janata Party had consistently won here
